<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Marsch für des Königs Leibwache No.1
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Gerson,_Georg" title="Category:Gerson, Georg">Gerson, Georg</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>G.85
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IGG 115
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>E-flat major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1814-11-25
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>2015-06-01
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1815 - Copenhagen: C.C. Lose (piano arr.)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>military band</i> <span class="expandline">
<dl><dd>E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span> flute, 2 oboes, E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span> clarinet, 2 clarinets (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>), 2 bassoons<br />4 horns (2 in E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>, 2 in B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>), 3 trumpets (2 in E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>, 1 in B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>),<br />bass trombone, serpant, corno basso*, triangle, bass drum <br />*<small>The <i>corno basso</i> was developed from the serpent around 1800. See <i>Handbuch der Musikinstrumentenkunde</i><br />by Curt Sachs (Leipzig, 1930. pp.264ff) and the German language <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/de:Basshorn" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:de:Basshorn">Wikipedia article on Basshorn</a>.</small> </span>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Performed at the return to Copenhagen of the Danish king, <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frederick_VI_of_Denmark" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Frederick VI of Denmark">Frederick VI</a> (1768-1839) from his participation in the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Congress_of_Vienna" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Congress of Vienna">Congress of Vienna</a> (1814-1815). The outcome of the congress was by no means as glorious for the Danish kingdom as the mood of Gerson's entry march. During the Congress of Vienna the German sovereigns, incl. Frederick VI as Duke of Holstein had promised <i>Stænderforsamlinger</i> (estate assemblies). In the end the Danes got spies and agent provocateurs only. See <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://rubicon.sdu.dk/assets/Blade/2010/rubicon-2010-4.pdf">Rasmus Glenthøj, Enevældens legitimitet, forandring og forfald, <i>Rubicon, Vol.4</i> (2010, pp.47 ff)</a>.
</td></tr></table>
</div>
